01 49775 3 LAB S P 0/20 W 1800-2045 08/24/16-12/12/16 ENG 339 --BIOLOGY UGRD: Important information for those students needing to take BIOL 1A/1B for Fall 2016: BIOL 1A/1B will be replaced by BIOL 30 and 31 effective AY 2016-2017. Those students needing to take BIOL 1A must enroll in BIOL 30 for Fall 2016 and then subsequently enroll in BIOL 31. Those students who have already passed BIOL 1A must now enroll in BIOL 30 to complete the former BIOL 1A/1B core sequence. Those students who have not passed BIOL 1A and seek grade forgiveness, must take BIOL 30 and then enroll in BIOL 31 to complete the core sequence. Please contact COSAC or the Biology Office for more information. BIOL 30 and 31, only the following majors may preregister: Biological Science, Forensic Science, Environmental Studies, Kinesiology, Biochemistry, Nutritional Science, Computer Science, Meteorology, and Communicative Disorders and Science. All other majors can enroll the first day of class if pre-and co-requisites are met. See catalog for details. For help in BIOL 10 see EDCO 10 listings for adjunct classes. BIOL 21 students can register for any laboratory section and must attend one lab each week (DH 448); the lab is a drop-in type and the open lab times will be announced at the first lecture meeting. pattern but has one optional on-campus meeting towards the end of the semester to discuss the final exam. ENVS 154 has mandatory field trips during class time and may return late some days. ENVS 166 has six (6) Sunday field trips. ENVS 181 has three sections offered for 01, 02, and 03 units all at the same class time. ENVS 185 requires an additional two (2) hours per week outside of class time for activity. During the semester, students will attend government meetings and satisfy service-learning. ENVS 187 requires six (6) Saturday field trips. ENVS 193 units are used for the Center for the Development of Recycling. Students may enroll for 01-06 units. Students create individual service-learning (work) schedules with the approval of the CDR Director, in addition for four class meetings during the semester. ENVS/ HUM/AMS 159 sec 01: students are required to attend weekly webinars on Sundays from 6:00 - 8:45 PM. Mandatory attendance at first and all online sessions to remain in class. GRAD: ENVS 210 has three sections offered for 01, 02, and 03 units all at the same time. ENVS 001 INTRO ENVIRON ISS 01 45561 3 LEC D3 70 P 119/120 TR 1330-1445 08/24/16-12/12/16 WSQ 207 J DOUGLAS ITAL 001A to be offered in Fall 2016 and ITAL 001B to be offered in Spring 2017. Course objectives are to induce the students to the fundamentals of Italian grammar so that after one year of study the student will be able to translate and engage in texts excerpted from Italian songs or opera, rather than literature or newspaper, with only a grammar and dictionary as aids. Contact michele.santamaria@sjsu.edu with questions. ITAL 001A ELEM ITALIAN 01 40203 5 SEM 113 05 20/24 MW 1200-1340 08/24/16-12/12/16 HB 405 M SANTAMARIA TBA TBA 08/24/16-12/12/16 TBA TBA ITAL 180 IND STUDIES 01 50333 3 SUP P 1/5 TBA TBA 08/24/16-12/12/16 M SANTAMARIA JAPANESE UGRD: JPN 001A, JPN 001B, JPN 025A, or JPN 025B (one course only) may be used for GE credit (Area C2). beginning level courses for students who wish to learn Latin. LATN 001A to be offered in Fall 2016 and LATN 001B to be offered in Spring 2017. Course objectives are to introduce the student to the fundamentals of Latin grammar so that after one year of study the student will be able to translate Latin texts from any period of Latin literature with only a grammar and dictionary as aids. Contact Michele. santamaria@sjsu.edu with questions. LINGUISTICS LING 020 NATURE OF LANGUAGE 01 42445 3 LEC D1 P 30/30 MW 1200-1315 08/24/16-12/12/16 BBC 221 C DONLAY LING 020 NATURE OF LANGUAGE For information, please contact aurelio.diasferreira@sjsu.edu. SPAN 001A, SPAN 001B, SPAN 025A, or SPAN 25B (up to two of these courses) can be used to satisfy Area C2 lower division GE requirements. SPAN 102B sections 01 & 02 are taught in Spanish; Section 03 is in English. All sections of SPAN 102B can be used for SJSU Studies Area V GE credit. Students Registration for SPAN 102B requires a passing score on the WST or successful completion of ENGL 100A or LLD 100A. Spanish Minors and Majors must take 102B in Spanish. SPAN 132 courses taught online are only open to students in the Graduate Program in Library Science. They require consent for the School of Information (formerly SLIS) for registration and are not open to WLL students. GRAD: SPAN 210 Seminar on Contemporary Spanish Literature and Culture. For advising contact eleanor.marsh@sjsu.edu or cheyla.samuelson@sjsu.edu. SPAN 001A ELEM SPANISH 01 45068 4 LEC C2 P 30/30 MW 1500-1640 08/24/16-12/12/16 CL 308 B RENTERIA MORAN SPAN 001A ELEM
